

#include <nvrtc.h>
#include <cuda.h>
#include <iostream>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <math.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <algorithm>


#define NUM_THREADS 256
#define NUM_BLOCKS 32

#define NUM_CUDA_CORES ( NUM_BLOCKS * NUM_THREADS )


#define NSTPT 3

#define NUM_X_ITER 351
#define NUM_Y_ITER 351
#define NUM_Z_ITER 351
#define NUM_T_ITER 701
#define SZ_T ( NSTPT * 2 + 1 )


#define MULTIPLIER_Y ( NUM_X_ITER )

#define MULTIPLIER_Z ( MULTIPLIER_Y * NUM_Y_ITER )

#define MULTIPLIER_T ( MULTIPLIER_Z * NUM_Z_ITER )

#define NUM_ITER_XYZ ( NUM_X_ITER * NUM_Y_ITER * NUM_Z_ITER )

#define NUM_ITER_XYZT ( NUM_ITER_XYZ * SZ_T )



#define HALF_X ( NUM_X_ITER / 2 )

#define HALF_Y ( NUM_Y_ITER / 2 )

#define HALF_Z ( NUM_Z_ITER / 2 )


#define RAD_X ( NUM_X_ITER / 10.0 )

#define RAD_Y ( NUM_Y_ITER / 10.0 )

#define RAD_Z ( NUM_Z_ITER / 10.0 )



#define NVRTC_SAFE_CALL(x) \
{ \
nvrtcResult result = x; \
if(result != NVRTC_SUCCESS) { \
std::cerr << "\nerror: " #x " failed with error " \
<< nvrtcGetErrorString(result) << '\n'; \
exit(1); \
} \
}



#define CUDA_SAFE_CALL(x) \
{ \
CUresult result = x; \
if(result != CUDA_SUCCESS) { \
const char *msg; \
cuGetErrorName(result, &msg); \
std::cerr << "\nerror: " #x " failed with error " \
<< msg << '\n'; \
exit(1); \
} \
}



class DblEnt
{

protected:

double val;

public:

DblEnt() {}

double& getVal()
{
   return(val);
}

void setVal( double in )
{
   val = in;
}

void negate( DblEnt& out )
{
   out.val = -( val );
}

void add( DblEnt& b , DblEnt& out )
{
   out.val = val + b.val;
}

void mult( DblEnt& b , DblEnt& out )
{
   out.val = val * b.val;
}

void invert( DblEnt& out )
{
   out.val = 1.0 / val;
}

void divideBy( const double d , DblEnt& out )
{
   out.val = val / d;
}


};


class CplxEnt
{

protected:

DblEnt re;
DblEnt im;

public:

CplxEnt() {}

DblEnt& getRe()
{
return(re);
}

DblEnt& getIm()
{
return(im);
}

void negate( CplxEnt& out )
{
   re.negate( out.re );
   im.negate( out.im );
}

void add( CplxEnt& b , CplxEnt& out )
{
   re.add( b.re , out.re );
   im.add( b.im , out.im );
}

void mult( CplxEnt& b , CplxEnt& out )
{
   DblEnt rere;
   re.mult( b.re , rere );
   DblEnt reim;
   re.mult( b.im , reim );
   DblEnt imre;
   im.mult( b.re , imre );
   DblEnt imim;
   im.mult( b.im , imim );
   DblEnt imimneg;
   imim.negate( imimneg );
   rere.add( imimneg , out.re );
   reim.add( imre , out.im );
}

void invert( CplxEnt& out )
{
   DblEnt resq;
   re.mult( re , resq );
   DblEnt imsq;
   im.mult( im , imsq );
   DblEnt denom;
   resq.add( imsq , denom );
   DblEnt div;
   denom.invert( div );
   re.mult( div , out.re );
   DblEnt imneg;
   im.negate( imneg );
   imneg.mult( div , out.im );
}

void divideBy( const double d , CplxEnt& out )
{
   re.divideBy( d , out.re );
   im.divideBy( d , out.im );
}


};



#define ARRAY_SIZE ( NUM_ITER_XYZT * sizeof(CplxEnt) )

__device__ size_t calcIdx( const size_t x , const size_t y , const size_t z , const size_t t ) \n\
{ \n\
return( x + y * MULTIPLIER_Y + z * MULTIPLIER_Z + t * MULTIPLIER_T ); \n\
} \n\
\
\
__device__ void fillTempArrayInner( CplxEnt* arr , const int tt , const size_t xv , const size_t yv , const size_t zv , const int tv , CplxEnt& out ) \n\
{ \n\
double avRe = 0.0; \n\
double avIm = 0.0; \n\
const double dx = ( (double) xv - HALF_X ) / RAD_X; \n\
const double dy = ( (double) yv - HALF_Y ) / RAD_Y; \n\
const double dz = ( (double) zv - HALF_Z ) / RAD_Z; \n\
if( (double) xv < XSST ) \n\
{ \n\
	avRe = DSSX * cos( ERATE * tv / NUM_T_ITER ); \n\
	avIm = DSSX * sin( ERATE * tv / NUM_T_ITER ); \n\
} \n\
else if( dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz < 1.0 ) \n\
{ \n\
	avRe = DSSX * cos( ERATE * tv / NUM_T_ITER ); \n\
	avIm = DSSX * sin( ERATE * tv / NUM_T_ITER ); \n\
} \n\
else \n\
{ \n\
        const int tdel = tt - tv; \n\
	if( ( tdel >= 0 ) && ( tdel < SZ_T ) && ( xv < NUM_X_ITER ) && ( yv < NUM_Y_ITER ) && ( zv < NUM_Z_ITER )  ) \n\
	{ \n\
		out = arr[ calcIdx( xv , yv , zv , tdel ) ]; \n\
		return; \n\
	} \n\
} \n\
out.getRe().setVal( avRe ); \n\
out.getIm().setVal( avIm ); \n\
} \n\
\n\

\n\
\n\
__device__ void evalPartialDerivative( CplxEnt* arr , const int tt , const size_t x , const size_t y , const size_t z , CplxEnt& out ) \
{ \n\
\n\
const double t_5054 = -3.7498769523010075E-13; fsfsfsdfsdfsdfs \n\
const double t_5055 = 0.0; sdfdsfsfdsfsdfdsfsdf \n\
const double t_5056 = 3.1250000000000005E-8; \n\
const double t_5057 = 0.0; \n\
const double t_5058 = 0.005; \n\
const double t_5059 = 0.0; \n\
const double t_5060 = t_5056 * t_5058 - t_5057 * t_5059; \n\
const double t_5061 = t_5056 * t_5059 + t_5057 * t_5058; \n\
const double t_5062 = t_5060 * t_5060 + t_5061 * t_5061; \n\
const double t_5063 = t_5060 / t_5062; \n\
const double t_5064 = - t_5061 / t_5062; \n\
const double t_5065 = t_5054 * t_5063 - t_5055 * t_5064; \n\
const double t_5066 = t_5054 * t_5064 + t_5055 * t_5063; \n\
out.getRe().setVal( t_5065 ); \n\
out.getIm().setVal( t_5066 ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ bool isnormal( const double in ) \n\
{ \n\
	return( !isnan( in ) && isfinite( in ) ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ bool iterationsDone( int& intCnt ) \n\
{ \n\
   intCnt++; \n\
   return( intCnt > 20 ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ int getMaxIterationsBacktrack( ) \n\
{ \n\
   return( 100 ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void cacheIterationValue( CplxEnt& p , CplxEnt& iterationValueCache ) \n\
{ \n\
   iterationValueCache = p; \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void retrieveIterationValue( CplxEnt& p , CplxEnt& iterationValueCache ) \n\
{ \n\
   p = iterationValueCache; \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void performIterationUpdate( CplxEnt& iterationOffset , CplxEnt& p ) \n\
{ \n\
   CplxEnt tmp; \n\
   p.add( iterationOffset , tmp ); \n\
   p = tmp; \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ bool evalIterationImproved( CplxEnt& lastValue , CplxEnt& nextValue ) \n\
{ \n\
	const double distLast = ( lastValue.getRe().getVal() ) * ( lastValue.getRe().getVal() ) + ( lastValue.getIm().getVal() ) * ( lastValue.getIm().getVal() ); \n\
	const double distNext = ( nextValue.getRe().getVal() ) * ( nextValue.getRe().getVal() ) + ( nextValue.getIm().getVal() ) * ( nextValue.getIm().getVal() ); \n\
	return( distNext < distLast ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void evalIndicatesImprovement( CplxEnt* arr , const int tt , const size_t x , const size_t y , const size_t z , CplxEnt& lastValue , CplxEnt& out ) \n\
{ \n\
CplxEnt ev; \n\
evalValue( arr , tt , x , y , z , ev ); \n\
\n\
if( !( evalIterationImproved( lastValue , ev ) ) ) \n\
{ \n\
        const double dval = sqrt( -1.0 ); // Means for generating NaN, since NaN function doesn't seem to work. \n\
	ev.getRe().setVal( dval ); \n\
	ev.getIm().setVal( dval ); \n\
} \n\
out = ev; \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void performIteration(CplxEnt* arr , const int tval , const size_t x , const size_t y , const size_t z , CplxEnt& p , \n\
CplxEnt& lastValue , CplxEnt& iterationValueCache , bool& iterationsStopped \n\
)  \n\
{ \n\
CplxEnt derivative; \n\
evalPartialDerivative( arr , tval , x , y , z , derivative ); \n\
\n\
CplxEnt derivativeInverse; \n\
\n\
derivative.invert( derivativeInverse ); \n\
if( !isnormal( derivativeInverse.getRe().getVal() ) || !isnormal( derivativeInverse.getIm().getVal() ) ) \n\
{ \n\
	return; \n\
} \n\
\n\
CplxEnt valueDivDerivative; \n\
lastValue.mult( derivativeInverse , valueDivDerivative ); \n\
CplxEnt iterationOffset; \n\
valueDivDerivative.negate( iterationOffset ); \n\
\n\
cacheIterationValue( p , iterationValueCache); \n\
\n\
performIterationUpdate( iterationOffset , p ); \n\
\n\
CplxEnt nextValue; \n\
evalIndicatesImprovement( arr , tval , x , y , z , lastValue , nextValue ); \n\
if( isnormal( nextValue.getRe().getVal() ) && isnormal( nextValue.getIm().getVal() ) ) \n\
{ \n\
	lastValue = nextValue; \n\
} \n\
else \n\
{ \n\
	int cnt = getMaxIterationsBacktrack(); \n\
	while( ( cnt > 0 ) && ( !isnormal( nextValue.getRe().getVal() ) || !isnormal( nextValue.getIm().getVal() ) ) ) \n\
	{ \n\
		cnt--; \n\
\n\
		CplxEnt tmp; \n\
		iterationOffset.divideBy( 2 , tmp ); \n\
		iterationOffset = tmp; \n\
\n\
		retrieveIterationValue( p , iterationValueCache ); \n\
\n\
		performIterationUpdate( iterationOffset , p ); \n\
\n\
		evalIndicatesImprovement( arr , tval , x , y , z , lastValue , nextValue ); \n\
	} \n\
	if( isnormal( nextValue.getRe().getVal() ) && isnormal( nextValue.getIm().getVal() ) ) \n\
	{ \n\
		lastValue = nextValue; \n\
	} \n\
	else \n\
	{ \n\
		// No suitable iteration can be found. \n\
		retrieveIterationValue( p , iterationValueCache ); \n\
		evalValue( arr , tval ,  x , y , z , lastValue ); \n\
		iterationsStopped = true; \n\
	} \n\
} \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void eval_newton(CplxEnt* arr , const int tval , const size_t x , const size_t y , const size_t z , CplxEnt& p , \n\
CplxEnt& iterationValueCache \n\
)  \n\
{ \n\
int intCnt = 0; \n\
bool iterationsStopped = false; \n\
CplxEnt lastValue; \n\
evalValue( arr , tval ,  x , y , z , lastValue ); \n\
while( !( iterationsDone( intCnt ) ) && !iterationsStopped ) \n\
{ \n\
	performIteration( arr , tval , x , y , z , p , lastValue , iterationValueCache , iterationsStopped ); \n\
} \n\
// return( lastValue ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
/** \n\
* Approximate maximum change allowed by nonlinear viscosity. \n\
*/ \n\
#define MAX_CHG 10000.0 \n\
\n\
/** \n\
* Multiplicative inverse of MAX_CHG. \n\
*/ \n\
#define I_MAX_CHG 1.0 / MAX_CHG \n\
\n\
/** \n\
* Size of change below which numerical viscosity isn't applied. \n\
*/ \n\
#define NUMERICAL_VISCOSITY_EXIT_CUTOFF 20.0 \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void applyNumericViscosityRe(CplxEnt* arr , const int tval , const size_t x , const size_t y , const size_t z , CplxEnt& p) \n\
{ \n\
		CplxEnt pim; \n\
		fillTempArrayInner( arr , tval , x   , y  , z  , tval  - 1 , pim ); \n\
		const double delt = p.getRe().getVal() \n\
			- pim.getRe().getVal(); \n\
		const double adelt = fabs( delt ); \n\
		if( adelt < NUMERICAL_VISCOSITY_EXIT_CUTOFF ) \n\
		{ \n\
			return; \n\
		} \n\
		const double iadelt = 1.0 / adelt; \n\
		const double iadiv = pow( iadelt * iadelt + I_MAX_CHG * I_MAX_CHG , 0.5 ); \n\
		const double adiv = 1.0 / iadiv; \n\
		p.getRe().setVal( \n\
				pim.getRe().getVal() + \n\
				( delt > 0.0 ? adiv : -adiv ) ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void applyNumericViscosityIm(CplxEnt* arr , const int tval , const size_t x , const size_t y , const size_t z , CplxEnt& p) \n\
{ \n\
	CplxEnt pim; \n\
	fillTempArrayInner( arr , tval , x   , y  , z  , tval  - 1 , pim ); \n\
	const double delt = p.getIm().getVal() \n\
		- pim.getIm().getVal(); \n\
	const double adelt = fabs( delt ); \n\
	if( adelt < NUMERICAL_VISCOSITY_EXIT_CUTOFF ) \n\
	{ \n\
		return; \n\
	} \n\
	const double iadelt = 1.0 / adelt; \n\
	const double iadiv = pow( iadelt * iadelt + I_MAX_CHG * I_MAX_CHG , 0.5 ); \n\
	const double adiv = 1.0 / iadiv; \n\
	p.getIm().setVal( \n\
			pim.getIm().getVal() + \n\
			( delt > 0.0 ? adiv : -adiv ) ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
__device__ void applyNumericViscosity(CplxEnt* arr , const int tval , const size_t x , const size_t y , const size_t z , CplxEnt& p) \n\
{ \n\
	applyNumericViscosityRe(arr, tval, x, y, z, p); \n\
	applyNumericViscosityIm(arr, tval, x, y, z, p); \n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
extern \"C\" __global__ \n\
void calcUpdate(int tval, double *outx)  \n\
{ \n\
const size_t tid = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x; \n\
\n\
CplxEnt* arr = (CplxEnt*) outx; \n\
\n\
for( size_t i = tid ; i < NUM_ITER_XYZ ; i += NUM_CUDA_CORES ) \n\
{ \n\
\n\
const size_t z = i / MULTIPLIER_Z; \n\
const size_t zz = i % MULTIPLIER_Z; \n\
const size_t y = zz / MULTIPLIER_Y; \n\
const size_t x = zz % MULTIPLIER_Y; \n\
\n\
CplxEnt& p = arr[ i ]; \n\
\n\
if( i != calcIdx( x , y , z , 0 ) ) return; \n\
\n\
CplxEnt iterationValueCache; \n\
const double dx = ( (double) x - HALF_X ) / RAD_X; \n\
const double dy = ( (double) y - HALF_Y ) / RAD_Y; \n\
const double dz = ( (double) z - HALF_Z ) / RAD_Z; \n\
if( (double) x < XSST ) \n\
{ \n\
        // Next two lines equivalent to resetCorrectionValue() \n\
	p.getRe().setVal( DSSX * cos( ERATE * tval / NUM_T_ITER ) ); \n\
	p.getIm().setVal( DSSX * sin( ERATE * tval / NUM_T_ITER ) ); \n\
        cacheIterationValue( p , iterationValueCache ); \n\
} \n\
else if( dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz < 1.0 ) \n\
{ \n\
        // Next two lines equivalent to resetCorrectionValue() \n\
	p.getRe().setVal( DSSX * cos( ERATE * tval / NUM_T_ITER ) ); \n\
	p.getIm().setVal( DSSX * sin( ERATE * tval / NUM_T_ITER ) ); \n\
        cacheIterationValue( p , iterationValueCache ); \n\
} \n\
else \n\
{ \n\
	eval_newton(arr , tval , x , y , z , p , iterationValueCache ); \n\
} \n\
\n\
if( APPLY_NUMERICAL_VISCOSITY ) \n\
{\n\
	applyNumericViscosity(arr , tval , x , y , z , p);\n\
}\n\
\n\
\n\
} \n\
\n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
extern \"C\" __global__ \n\
void initIterArray( double *outx ) \n\
{ \n\
const size_t tid = blockIdx.x * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x; \n\
\n\
CplxEnt* arr = (CplxEnt*) outx; \n\
\n\
for( size_t i = tid ; i < NUM_ITER_XYZT ; i += NUM_CUDA_CORES ) \n\
{ \n\
const size_t t = i / MULTIPLIER_T; \n\
const size_t tt = i % MULTIPLIER_T; \n\
const size_t z = tt / MULTIPLIER_Z; \n\
const size_t zz = tt % MULTIPLIER_Z; \n\
const size_t y = zz / MULTIPLIER_Y; \n\
const size_t x = zz % MULTIPLIER_Y; \n\
\n\
CplxEnt& p = arr[ i ]; \n\
\n\
const double dx = ( (double) x - HALF_X ) / RAD_X; \n\
const double dy = ( (double) y - HALF_Y ) / RAD_Y; \n\
const double dz = ( (double) z - HALF_Z ) / RAD_Z; \n\
const int tcnt = 1 - t; \n\
\n\
if( (double) x < XSST ) \n\
{ \n\
	p.getRe().setVal( DSSX * cos( ERATE * tcnt / NUM_T_ITER ) ); \n\
	p.getIm().setVal( DSSX * sin( ERATE * tcnt / NUM_T_ITER ) ); \n\
} \n\
else \n\
{ \n\
	if( dx * dx + dy * dy + dz * dz < 1.0 ) \n\
	{ \n\
		p.getRe().setVal( DSSX * cos( ERATE * tcnt / NUM_T_ITER + EPHASEB ) ); \n\
		p.getIm().setVal( DSSX * sin( ERATE * tcnt / NUM_T_ITER + EPHASEB ) ); \n\
	} \n\
	else \n\
	{ \n\
		p.getRe().setVal( 0.0 ); \n\
		p.getIm().setVal( 0.0 ); \n\
	} \n\
} \n\
\n\
} \n\
\n\
} \n\
\n\
\n\
\n";






#define OUT_FILEPATH "/d/outdir/outD_"





double changeEndian(double in)
{
	char* const p = reinterpret_cast<char*>(&in);
	for(size_t i = 0; i < sizeof(double) / 2; ++i)
		std::swap(p[i], p[sizeof(double) - i - 1] );
	return in;
}





void storeValues( int tcnt , double* hOut , double* writeBuffer )
{
	double maxD = 0.0;
	printf( "Writing %d\n" , tcnt );
	const int CNTR_IDX = 2 * ( HALF_X + HALF_Y * MULTIPLIER_Y + HALF_Z * MULTIPLIER_Z );
	for( int cnt = 0 ; cnt < 2 * NUM_ITER_XYZ ; cnt++ )
	{
		const double dd = hOut[ cnt ];
		if( isfinite( dd ) && !isnan( dd ) )
		{
			const double dd2 = changeEndian( dd );
			writeBuffer[ cnt ] = dd2;
			if( abs( dd ) > abs( maxD ) )
			{
				maxD = dd;
				const size_t t = ( cnt / 2 ) / MULTIPLIER_T;
				const size_t tt = ( cnt / 2 ) % MULTIPLIER_T;
				const size_t z = tt / MULTIPLIER_Z;
				const size_t zz = tt % MULTIPLIER_Z;
				const size_t y = zz / MULTIPLIER_Y;
				const size_t x = zz % MULTIPLIER_Y;
				printf( "Coord : %d %d %d %d \n" , (int) t , (int) z , (int) y , (int) x );
				printf( "maxD : %lf\n" , maxD );
			}
			/* if( cnt == 0 ) printf( "0 Res: %le %le\n" , dd , dd2 );
			if( cnt == 1 ) printf( "1 Res: %le %le\n" , dd , dd2 );
			if( cnt == CNTR_IDX )
			{
				printf( "C0 Res: %le %le\n" , dd , dd2 );
				const size_t t = ( cnt / 2 ) / MULTIPLIER_T;
				const size_t tt = ( cnt / 2 ) % MULTIPLIER_T;
				const size_t z = tt / MULTIPLIER_Z;
				const size_t zz = tt % MULTIPLIER_Z;
				const size_t y = zz / MULTIPLIER_Y;
				const size_t x = zz % MULTIPLIER_Y;
				printf( "Coord: %d %d %d %d \n" , (int) t , (int) z , (int) y , (int) x );
				const double dx = ( (double) x - HALF_X ) / RAD_X;
				const double dy = ( (double) y - HALF_Y ) / RAD_Y;
				const double dz = ( (double) z - HALF_Z ) / RAD_Z;
				printf( "dx: %le %le %le \n" , dx , dy , dz );
			}
			if( cnt == CNTR_IDX + 1 ) printf( "C1 Res: %le %le\n" , dd , dd2 ); */
		}
		else
		{
			printf( "Nan Detected In Result.  Exiting. %d  %d\n\n" , cnt , cnt / 2 );
			std::cout << dd << '\n' << '\n';
			std::cout << isnormal( dd ) << '\n' << '\n';
			std::cout << isnan( dd ) << '\n' << '\n';
			std::cout << isfinite( dd ) << '\n' << '\n';
			exit( 1 );
		}
	}
	char fname[ 255 ];
	sprintf( fname , "%s%d" , OUT_FILEPATH , tcnt );
	FILE* fo = fopen( fname , "w" );
        if( fwrite( writeBuffer , 1 , NUM_ITER_XYZ * sizeof(CplxEnt) , fo ) != NUM_ITER_XYZ * sizeof(CplxEnt) )
	{
		printf( "Write Fail Error" );
		exit( 1 );
	}
        fclose( fo );
	printf( "Written %d\n" , tcnt );
}






/**
 * Gets the expected number of CUDA cores.
 * Copied from https://stackoverflow.com/questions/32530604/how-can-i-get-number-of-cores-in-cuda-device
 */
int getSPcores( int mp , int devPropMajor , int devPropMinor )
{
   int cores = 0;
   switch( devPropMajor )
   {
   	  case 2: // Fermi
   		 if ( devPropMinor == 1 ) cores = mp * 48;
   	     else cores = mp * 32;
	     break;
      case 3: // Kepler
         cores = mp * 192;
         break;
      case 5: // Maxwell
    	  cores = mp * 128;
    	  break;
      case 6: // Pascal
        if ( ( devPropMinor == 1 ) || ( devPropMinor == 2 ) ) cores = mp * 128;
        else if ( devPropMinor == 0 ) cores = mp * 64;
        else  printf( "Unknown Device\n" );
        break;
      case 7: // Volta and Turing
    	  if ( ( devPropMinor == 0 ) || ( devPropMinor == 5 ) ) cores = mp * 64;
    	  else  printf( "Unknown Device\n" );
    	  break;
      case 8: // Ampere
    	  if ( devPropMinor == 0 ) cores = mp * 64;
    	  else if ( devPropMinor == 6 ) cores = mp * 128;
    	  else  printf( "Unknown Device\n" );
    	  break;
      default:
         printf( "Unknown Device\n" );
         break;
   }
   return( cores );
}





int main(void)
{

   printf( "Hello World\n" );


   nvrtcProgram prog;


  NVRTC_SAFE_CALL(
     nvrtcCreateProgram(
         &prog, // prog
         calcUpdate, // buffer
         "calcUpdate.cu" , // name
         0 , // numHeaders
         NULL , // headers
         NULL ) // includeNames
);


   printf( "Created Program\n" );



   const char* opts[] = { "--fmad=false" };
   nvrtcResult compileResult = nvrtcCompileProgram(
       prog, // prog
      1, // numOptions
      opts ); // options


   printf( "Compiled Program\n" );


   size_t logSize;
   NVRTC_SAFE_CALL(
      nvrtcGetProgramLogSize( prog , &logSize ) );
   char *log = new char[logSize];
   NVRTC_SAFE_CALL( nvrtcGetProgramLog( prog, log ) );
   std::cout << log << '\n';
   delete[] log;
   if( compileResult != NVRTC_SUCCESS )
       { exit(1); }



   printf( "Generated Compile Log\n" );


   // Obtain the PTX from the program.
   size_t ptxSize;
   NVRTC_SAFE_CALL( nvrtcGetPTXSize( prog , &ptxSize ) );
   char* ptx = new char[ ptxSize ];
   NVRTC_SAFE_CALL( nvrtcGetPTX( prog, ptx) );
   NVRTC_SAFE_CALL( nvrtcDestroyProgram( &prog ) );



   printf( "Obtained PTX\n" );



   // Load the generated PTX and get a handle to the calcUpdate kernel.
   CUdevice cuDevice;
   CUcontext context;
   CUmodule module;

   CUfunction kernelInitIterArray;
   CUfunction kernelCalcUpdate;

   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuInit(0) );
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuDeviceGet( &cuDevice, 0) );


   // Sanity check to make sure enough space is available
   size_t deviceBytes;
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuDeviceTotalMem( &deviceBytes , cuDevice ) );
   const size_t deviceChunks = deviceBytes / ( SZ_T * sizeof( CplxEnt ) );
   std::cout << "AppxSz : " << pow( deviceChunks , 1.0 / 3.0 ) << std::endl;
   std::cout << "AppxSz (80%) : " << 0.8 * pow( deviceChunks / 2 , 1.0 / 3.0 ) << std::endl;
   if( deviceChunks < NUM_ITER_XYZ )
   {
      printf( "Memory Pre-Check Says Fail.\n" );
      exit( 1 );
   }


   int multiProcessorCount;
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuDeviceGetAttribute( &multiProcessorCount , CU_DEVICE_ATTRIBUTE_MULTIPROCESSOR_COUNT , cuDevice ) );
   std::cout << "MultiProcessorCount : " << multiProcessorCount << std::endl;


   int devMajor;
   int devMinor;
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuDeviceComputeCapability( &devMajor , &devMinor , cuDevice ) );
   std::cout << "devMajor : " << devMajor << std::endl;
   int spCores = getSPcores( multiProcessorCount , devMajor , devMinor );
   std::cout << "SPCores : " << NUM_CUDA_CORES << " / " << spCores << std::endl;


   printf( "Initializing Cuda Function Load.\n" );


   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuCtxCreate( &context, 0, cuDevice) );
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuModuleLoadDataEx( &module, ptx, 0, 0, 0 ) );
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuModuleGetFunction( &kernelInitIterArray , module , "initIterArray" ) );
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuModuleGetFunction( &kernelCalcUpdate , module , "calcUpdate" ) );


   printf( "Initialized Cuda Function Load.\n" );


   // Generate input for execution


   if( sizeof(CplxEnt) != 2 * sizeof(double) )
   {
      printf( "Size Mismatch" );
      exit(1);
   }

   printf( "Initializing Host-Side Array.\n" );

   size_t bufferSize = ARRAY_SIZE;
   CplxEnt *hOut = new CplxEnt[NUM_ITER_XYZT];


   printf( "Initialized Host-Side Array.\n" );


   if( hOut == NULL )
   {
       printf( "Out Of Memory" );
       exit(1);
   }


   CplxEnt *writeBuffer = new CplxEnt[NUM_ITER_XYZ];


   printf( "Initialized Write Buffer.\n" );


   if( writeBuffer == NULL )
   {
       printf( "Out Of Memory" );
       exit(1);
   }


   printf( "Started Initialization.\n" );


   CUdeviceptr dOut;


   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuMemAlloc( &dOut , 2 * bufferSize ) );



   // Execute initIterArray

   void *argsInitIterArray[] = { &dOut };

   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuLaunchKernel( kernelInitIterArray,
      NUM_BLOCKS, 1, 1,
      NUM_THREADS, 1, 1,
      0, NULL,
      argsInitIterArray, 0) );


   // Send back the entire initialized buffer.
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuMemcpyDtoH( (double*) hOut, dOut, bufferSize ) );


   // Store Results.
   storeValues( 0 , (double*) hOut , (double*) writeBuffer );



   printf( "Ended Initialization\n" );



   for( int tcnt = 1 ; tcnt < ( NUM_T_ITER - NSTPT ) /* 2 */ ; tcnt++ )
   {


   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuMemcpyHtoD( dOut , (double*) hOut , bufferSize ) );


   // Execute calcUpdate

   void *argsCalcUpdate[] = { &tcnt , &dOut };

   printf( "Starting Launch %d\n" , tcnt );

   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuLaunchKernel( kernelCalcUpdate,
      NUM_BLOCKS, 1, 1,
      NUM_THREADS, 1, 1,
      0, NULL,
      argsCalcUpdate, 0) );


   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuCtxSynchronize() );

   printf( "Ended Launch\n" );

   // Only Send the Result t=0 Row Back
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuMemcpyDtoH( (double*) hOut, dOut, NUM_ITER_XYZ * sizeof(CplxEnt) ) );


   // Store Results.
   storeValues( tcnt , (double*) hOut , (double*) writeBuffer );


   // Advance Array Elements
   for( int tt = SZ_T - 1 ; tt > 0 ; tt-- )
   {
      memcpy( (double*)( &( hOut[ tt * NUM_ITER_XYZ ] ) ) , (double*)( &( hOut[ ( tt - 1 ) * NUM_ITER_XYZ ] ) ) , NUM_ITER_XYZ * sizeof(CplxEnt) );
   }


   }


   printf( "Finished\n" );


   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuMemFree( dOut ) );
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuModuleUnload( module ) );
   CUDA_SAFE_CALL( cuCtxDestroy( context ) );
   delete[] hOut;

   return 0;


}
